    admin 管理者ページ

    api/admin/groups

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/admin/groups" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/admin/groups");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response:

    null

    HTTP Request

    GET api/attributes

    attributes.store 属性追加

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/attributes" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"name":"9Fw34D8GzhUZ6xNQ","plus_minus":2}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/attributes");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "name": "9Fw34D8GzhUZ6xNQ",
    "plus_minus": 2
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (201):

    HTTP Request

    POST api/attributes

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string required 属性名。必須
    plus_minus integer optional 加減算

    attributes.show 属性の一つの詳細を得る

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/attributes/{attribute}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/attributes/{attribute}");

    let params = {
            "attribute": "srAO4mndERpCtzIj",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/attributes/{attribute}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    attribute required 属性id

    attributes.update 対象の属性をアップデート

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/attributes/{attribute}" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"name":"iy0bip8vrGuv2Z3r","plus_minus":9}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/attributes/{attribute}");

    let params = {
            "attribute": "shJO7kY2B80aI9Tl",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "name": "iy0bip8vrGuv2Z3r",
    "plus_minus": 9
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/attributes/{attribute}

    PATCH api/attributes/{attribute}

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string required 属性名。必須
    plus_minus integer optional 加減算

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    attribute required 属性id

    attributes.destory 属性の削除

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/attributes/{attribute}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/attributes/{attribute}");

    let params = {
            "attribute": "UE7PhTbspogRfJgC",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (204):

    []

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/attributes/{attribute}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    attribute required 属性id

    auth 認証

    email, password, usernameでユーザー登録し、JWTを得る

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/auth/register" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"email":"8eaQtyo0bzseBlsq","username":"BWWTXyYeRaRH7mB2","password":"8gbkqPyr8QxHxvAh"}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/auth/register");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "email": "8eaQtyo0bzseBlsq",
    "username": "BWWTXyYeRaRH7mB2",
    "password": "8gbkqPyr8QxHxvAh"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {

    HTTP Request

    POST api/auth/register

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    email string required メールアドレス
    username string required ユーザーネーム（表示される名前）
    password string required パスワード

    email, password でログインし、JWTを得る

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/auth/login" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"email":"xRDHQr0o6W1V43YT","password":"DyMSHfV4l0tpM4PQ"}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/auth/login");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "email": "xRDHQr0o6W1V43YT",
    "password": "DyMSHfV4l0tpM4PQ"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "access_token": "eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJodHRwOlwvXC9sb2NhbGhvc3RcL2FwaVwvYXV0aFwvbG9naW4iLCJpYXQiOjE1NTA3MzY1NjUsImV4cCI6MTU1MDc0MDE2NSwibmJmIjoxNTUwNzM2NTY1LCJqdGkiOiJaU2U3NmZPa21MdWxrWUt3Iiwic3ViIjoyLCJwcnYiOiI4N2UwYWYxZWY5ZmQxNTgxMmZkZWM5NzE1M2ExNGUwYjA0NzU0NmFhIn0.Msm2W2gyqqm2a8jMEoqx9l7h5wmGkhdzMmcp6sxTVVc",
    "token_type": "bearer",
    "expires_in": 3600
}

    Example response (401):

    {
    "error": "Unauthorized"

            "default_setting": "CZEFdipmfnKQqglo",

    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "name": "h402EzOosDSbTz2B",
    "timer": 14,
    "group_id": 17
}

    method: "PUT",

})

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/default_settings/{default_setting}

    PATCH api/default_settings/{default_setting}

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string required 設定名
    timer integer required 始まるまでの時間'01:00:00'形式
    group_id integer required この設定を適用するグループid

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    default_setting required 設定のid

    default_settings.destroy 一つのデフォルト設定を削除する

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/default_settings/{default_setting}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/default_settings/{default_setting}");

    let params = {
            "default_setting": "zy2f1ZJmO3Cw7DW6",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (204):

    []

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/default_settings/{default_setting}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    default_setting required 設定のid

    friends 友達

    friends.index 友達一覧

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/friends" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/friends");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/friends

    friends.store 友達申請する

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/friends" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"email":"Xu0H0PKiJmRVs0Zi"}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/friends");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "email": "Xu0H0PKiJmRVs0Zi"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (201):

    {
    "id": 1,
    "unique_id": "TESTTEST",
    "name": null,

    POST api/friends

    HTTP Request

    GET api/friends/blocking

    friends.block_me_users 申請した中でブロックされているユーザー一覧

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/friends/block_me" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/friends/block_me");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/friends/waiting

    friends.permittingUsers 自分に申請してきたユーザーで、自分がそれを了承したユーザー（自分をフレンドとしているユーザー一覧）

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/friends/permitting" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/friends/permitting");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/friends/permitting

    friends.friendRequestUsers 自分に申請してきてるけど、まだ返事していない相手一覧

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/friends/requested" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/friends/requested");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/friends/requested

    friends.permit 友達申請を許可

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/friends/permit" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"user_id":15}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/friends/permit");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "user_id": 15
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "message": "招待を許可しました"
}

    Example response (409):

    {
    "error": "そのユーザーからは招待されていません"
}

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/groups/{group}

    PATCH api/groups/{group}

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string required 新たにつけるグループ名

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    group required グループid

    groups.destory グループを削除

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/groups/{group}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/groups/{group}");

    let params = {
            "group": "Hs3iuI3kHOwgV6va",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (204):

    []

    Example response (409):

    {
    "error": "このグループを使用しているデフォルト設定があるので、削除できません"
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/guest/sessions

    guests.sessions.show ゲストとして参加しているセッションの一つの詳細

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/guest/sessions/{session}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/guest/sessions/{session}");

    let params = {
            "session": "pR1V63e7DZrY5bka",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/guest/sessions/{session}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid

    guests.sessions.update セッション参加状況を更新する（join_statusのみ。allow, wait, denyの文字のみ。）

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/guest/sessions/{session}" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"join_status":"PKjmqZj89Rg1a1Qu"}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/guest/sessions/{session}");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "join_status": "PKjmqZj89Rg1a1Qu"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "data": {
        "id": 1,
        "unique_id": "TESTTEST",
        "name": null,
        "username": "テスト太郎",

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/guest/sessions/{session}

    PATCH api/guest/sessions/{session}

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    join_status string required 参加状況のステータス['allow', 'wait', 'deny']

    profile プロフィール

    profiles.update 自分の情報を更新

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/profile/update" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"unique_id":"36H4svEzXYTtWZPV","username":"Xb3RmUpjfVAMkZRG","password":"IWa0gHvFQYpMYktI","unique_id_search_flag":false,"username_search_flag":false}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/profile/update");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "unique_id": "36H4svEzXYTtWZPV",
    "username": "Xb3RmUpjfVAMkZRG",
    "password": "IWa0gHvFQYpMYktI",
    "unique_id_search_flag": false,
    "username_search_flag": false
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {

    unique_id string required

let headers = {

    HTTP Request

    GET api/search/can_add_friend_users

    search.forward_by_username ユーザーネームで検索し、複数を返す(前方一致)

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/search/forward_by_username" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"username":"kmXsoMaMwcaKP4FP"}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/search/forward_by_username");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "username": "kmXsoMaMwcaKP4FP"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "data": [
        {
            "id": 1,
            "unique_id": "TESTTEST",
            "name": null,
            "username": "テスト太郎",

            "username_search_flag": 1,

                "date": "2019-02-21 08:06:40.000000",

    HTTP Request

    let params = {
            "session": "jGIyZPkokrjcADC7",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/sessions/{session}/users

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid

    sessions.users.store セッションにユーザーを追加する

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"user_id":"e4Rw31zMzccQTjmi","join_status":"imkfusXiHlxXOzKv","paid":18,"plus_minus":6,"budget":17,"budget_actual":17}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users");

    let params = {
            "session": "iDXpiZvSedBs9Nhb",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "user_id": "e4Rw31zMzccQTjmi",
    "join_status": "imkfusXiHlxXOzKv",
    "paid": 18,
    "plus_minus": 6,
    "budget": 17,
    "budget_actual": 17
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "data": [
        {
            "id": 24,

    HTTP Request

    POST api/sessions/{session}/users

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    user_id string required 追加するユーザーのID
    join_status string required 参加状況のステータス['allow', 'wait', 'deny']
    paid integer optional 支払いしたか
    plus_minus integer optional 加減算
    budget integer optional 支払い予定額
    budget_actual integer optional 支払い確定金額

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid

    sessions.users.show セッションの中の一人のユーザーの詳細を得る（属性とか見たりするでしょう）

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}");

    let params = {
            "session": "d5C68NaUyMmzCxOD",
            "user": "UC19nXjB1C4oFo2t",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "data": {
        "id": 24,
        "unique_id": "W9q3wPojYu",

    HTTP Request

    GET api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid
    user required セッションに属するユーザーのid

    sessions.users.update セッションの中のユーザーのステータスなどを更新する

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"user_id":"5cfr1EBylkWAULSE","join_status":1,"paid":4,"plus_minus":5,"budget":6,"budget_actual":19}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}");

    let params = {
            "session": "kFwFOjhreeU38n7m",
            "user": "MJTWpU4IcIdbooWG",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "user_id": "5cfr1EBylkWAULSE",
    "join_status": 1,
    "paid": 4,
    "plus_minus": 5,
    "budget": 6,
    "budget_actual": 19
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (200):

    {
    "data": {
        "id": 13,

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}

    PATCH api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    user_id string optional 追加するユーザーのID
    join_status integer optional 参加状況のステータス
    paid integer optional 支払いしたか
    plus_minus integer optional 加減算
    budget integer optional 支払い予定額
    budget_actual integer optional 支払い確定金額

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid
    user required セッションに属するユーザーのid

    sessions.users.destory セッションからユーザーを削除する

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}");

    let params = {
            "session": "0UkmTJXR1k2nYfSp",
            "user": "u7NpD42SVoWk3eIJ",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (204):

    []

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/sessions/{session}/users/{user}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid
    user required セッションに属するユーザーのid

    session イベントセッション

    sessions.index 管理しているセッション一覧

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/sessions"

let headers = {

}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/sessions

    sessions.store セッションを作成

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/sessions" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"name":"zHpwWRSFDjqhcPrx","shop_id":"AFOAZ4v4FfRzowtZ","budget":7,"actual":6,"start_time":"v8xBkFybgzLRDD7R","end_time":"uyVLuPnnLg0MJTdp"}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions");

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "name": "zHpwWRSFDjqhcPrx",
    "shop_id": "AFOAZ4v4FfRzowtZ",
    "budget": 7,
    "actual": 6,
    "start_time": "v8xBkFybgzLRDD7R",
    "end_time": "uyVLuPnnLg0MJTdp"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (201):

    {
    "data": {
        "id": 201,
        "name": "newSessionotsQu",

    HTTP Request

    POST api/sessions

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string required 新規セッションの名前
    shop_id string optional ショップのID(ぐるなび？)
    budget integer optional 予算額
    actual integer optional 実際の金額
    start_time datetime optional セッションの開始時刻
    end_time datetime optional セッションの終了時刻

    sessions.show 一つのセッションの詳細

    Example request:

    curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}");

    let params = {
            "session": "cwCHuLZY0r7duFCQ",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    GET api/sessions/{session}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid

    sessions.update セッション情報を更新

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"name":"vZm0jts2zsUZ0viX","shop_id":19,"budget":4,"actual":15,"start_time":"a0p3JMoEEpQFa5Fm","end_time":"OJ3AEbBLoaV86ece"}'

    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}");

    let params = {
            "session": "7bAMbzs8PDwPKYUJ",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
}

let body = {
    "name": "vZm0jts2zsUZ0viX",
    "shop_id": 19,
    "budget": 4,
    "actual": 15,
    "start_time": "a0p3JMoEEpQFa5Fm",
    "end_time": "OJ3AEbBLoaV86ece"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
    body: body
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/sessions/{session}

    PATCH api/sessions/{session}

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string optional 新規セッションの名前
    shop_id integer optional ショップのID(ぐるなび？)
    budget integer optional 予算額
    actual integer optional 実際の金額
    start_time datetime optional セッションの開始時刻
    end_time datetime optional セッションの終了時刻

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid

    sessions.destory セッションを削除

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}" 
    const url = new URL("http://localhost/api/sessions/{session}");

    let params = {
            "session": "lMv8Ae6AQKWYolHb",
        };
    Object.keys(params).forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));

    Example response (204):

    []

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/sessions/{session}

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    session required セッションid
    bash javascript
